name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Couples
info:9 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:[A Thousand Words Dismantling the Hotel]
[Me and the Hotel] The reason for choosing Hangzhou Qiantang Puyan Hotel this time is simple: it‚Äôs cheap! There was no price increase during May Day! When Hanting, All Seasons, and Atour couldn't book a room for up to 500 to 600 yuan, the price of Hangzhou Qiantang Puyan Hotel on May 2nd was only about 400 yuan. I was a platinum member and got a free upgrade. . Although the hotel is in Xiasha, it is only 200 meters away from the Line 1 subway station. It is just across a shopping mall and can go directly to the city center without changing trains. If you don't want to go to the city center, there are three shopping malls near the hotel, which is really okay.
[Tips from check-in to check-out]
1. The hotel has free parking, both above ground and underground.
2. There are 4 elevators in the hotel, but because 2345 has a dining area, you sometimes have to wait.
3. Your face will be scanned when you check in. The face scan is just for the convenience of checking in. You don‚Äôt need to bring your room card with you during the whole process.
4. The room does not require a room card to get electricity. It is available when you open the door. However, you need to click "Welcome" to open the door, otherwise some jacks will be out of power. The lady at the front desk did not tell me about this, so I used it at the beginning. Electricity problem
5. I am not an art major, but the overall design style of the hotel is very avant-garde, with a new Chinese style, which is very attractive to young people. There is a lot of information and promotion on the Internet, so I won‚Äôt go into it here.
6. Everything is available in the room, including coffee capsules, smart voice, smart toilet, bathtub, etc. However, "Xiaodu" is a little hard of hearing and sometimes has to shout louder.
7. Complain about the TV. There is no prompt to turn off the TV. I have to put the remote control about 20 centimeters in front of the TV and align it to turn it off. As a result, I turned it off in bed for a long time.
8. The bathrobe is very comfortable, and the full-body shower facility is the first time I have seen it, which is very good. Now that we have a bathtub, how about putting an extra wooden board or somewhere in the bathtub for me to use my phone?
9. The socket was out of power, and the maintenance man called was very patient.
10. Let‚Äôs complain about the self-service laundry. The hotel has laundry facilities (charged) and self-service (free). The self-service laundry items are not as good as some budget hotels, including the quality of equipment and the type and quality of laundry detergent. Moreover, the self-service washing machine is on 20F. If I don‚Äôt Living on 20F, it seems that the regular elevator cannot go up (you can only go to the floor where you check in), so no one reminded me how to get up (I took the employee elevator myself).
11. I have not tried the catering facilities here, so I will not comment on them.
12. All the staff were very gentle. When they gave me the parking ticket when I left, they also reminded me that I must leave within 15 minutes after scanning the code.
13. The coffee cup of the coffee machine is too big. Go and try it. How much coffee can the coffee capsule produce? Do you need such a big coffee cup? It tastes weird to drink
[Final words]
   This is the first time I have stayed at a hotel under the Lichen Hotel Group. Lichen Hotel is backed by Ctrip and has done a good job in digital operations. I feel very good about this stay, but what is the digital operation behind it, including the hotel's finances? I am very curious about what it is like. It is said that the decoration cost of each hotel is about 150,000, which is comparable to Atour, but obviously the quality is much better than Atour. I don‚Äôt know how long it will take for such a hotel to be established. If there are more hotels like this, there really will be no Atour. Duo, what happened? One last thing to mention, if a guest leaves the room temporarily without clicking "Leave", it will seem like the electricity will be on all the time. This is certainly good for the guest, but is the hotel really that luxurious? Can't you save some electricity?
